17/06/21, 4:54 pm - Piiyush Senior Carerr Counselor: basically there are 3 phases of the enrollment process. 

*Phase 1: Counseling session with the Students/Parents and Seat Reservation*

If the student is found competent for the program and receives their Reservation Letter, you will have to pay only a part of the Program Fee which is $200 within 7 days from the receipt of your Edoofa Reservation Letter which basically is for the seat reservation and the Earn While You Learn Program.

*Phase 2:* Once the students complete their Phase 1 they will be starting their Earn While you Learn program classes (Each student will have an opportunity to earn credits that can be used to reduce the fee, before their A Level result is out).

*Phase 3:* Once the final A level results are out if the child would have passed the necessary requirement then in order to complete the enrollment process, the payment of the balance of $150 is to be done. If the child wouldn't have met the necessary requirements then the paid $200 would be refunded back to the parents. 

*The amount of credit earned by the students during Phase 2 can be used to adjust the fee and the balance is to be paid in that case*

06/09/21, 10:30 am - Shubham Madhwal: Hello Team, 
Just a reminder on how to handle seat reservation cases:

1. Since you will be interacting with the parents make sure to share the 3 phases for Seat Reservation.

2. After the parent is pitched make sure they understand the program well. And clear all their doubts

3. Connect the Parents with Abhinav sir for a Seat Reservation call
06/09/21, 10:30 am - Shubham Madhwal: *Phase 1: Counseling session with the Students/Parents and Seat Reservation*

If the student is found competent for the program and receives their Reservation Letter, you will have to pay only a part of the Program Fee which is $200 within 7 days from the receipt of your Edoofa Reservation Letter which basically is for the seat reservation and the Earn While You Learn Program.

*Phase 2:* Once the students complete their Phase 1 they will be starting their Earn While you Learn program classes (Each student will have an opportunity to earn credits that can be used to reduce the fee, before their A Level result is out).

*Phase 3:* Once the final A level results are out if the child would have passed the necessary requirement then in order to complete the enrollment process, the payment of the balance of $150 is to be done. If the child wouldn't have met the necessary requirements then the paid $200 would be refunded back to the parents. 

*The amount of credit earned by the students during Phase 2 can be used to adjust the fee and the balance is to be paid in that case*
